</th>

<td>scan: score scanned at 600dpi<br />filter: score filtered with 2-point algorithm explained in <a href="/wiki/IMSLP:High_Quality_Scanning" title="IMSLP:High Quality Scanning">High Quality Scanning</a><br />I provide the original scanned version and the filtered, because the filter does some changes (smoothening, sharpening borders) and some portions of the scan get lost sometimes (when they are too small e.g.) - so you can choose your favorite. You may ask me for a manually cleaned version.

</li><li> (E major)

<dl><dd><a href="/wiki/Category:Schumann,_Clara" title="Category:Schumann, Clara">Clara Schumann</a> and <a href="/wiki/Category:Dietrich,_Albert" title="Category:Dietrich, Albert" class="mw-redirect">Albert Dietrich</a> (piano)
</dd></dl>
<p>1867-3-17 in Vienna, Redoutensaal
</p>
<dl><dd>Stephanie Vrabely and Seraphine Tausig (pianos)
</dd></dl>

</p>
<dl><dd><a href="/wiki/Category:Brahms,_Johannes" title="Category:Brahms, Johannes">Johannes Brahms</a> (piano) – unknown number of selections.
</dd></dl>

<ul><li>Piano 4-hands, Plate 470, 33 pages
</li><li>Piano solo, Plates 524-525, 18 and 16 pages (concert and simplified)

</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Extra Information
</th>
<td>Version History
<ul><li> Composed for piano 4 hands, 1865
</li><li> Arranged for solo piano by Brahms, 1865, with keys of Nos. 13-16 shifted down a half-step (first performance in this version: Hamburg, 15 November 1868; first published in 1867)
</li><li> Nos.1, 2, 8, 11, 14, 15 were also arranged for 2 pianos by Brahms, 1867 (first performance in this version: Vienna, 17 March 1867; first published (except No.8) in 1897)
</li></ul>
</td></tr></table>
